from reportlab.platypus import SimpleDocTemplate, Paragraph, Spacer, Table, TableStyle, PageBreak
from reportlab.lib.styles import getSampleStyleSheet, ParagraphStyle
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import LETTER
from reportlab.lib import colors

file_path = "/mnt/data/PureTask_Cleaner_Onboarding_SOP_BW.pdf"
doc = SimpleDocTemplate(file_path, pagesize=LETTER, leftMargin=50, rightMargin=50, topMargin=40, bottomMargin=40)
styles = getSampleStyleSheet()
story = []

# Title Page
story.append(Paragraph("<b>PURETASK OPERATIONS MANUAL</b>", styles["Title"]))
story.append(Paragraph("Module 1 — Cleaner Verification & Compliance (Black & White Version)", styles["Heading2"]))
story.append(Spacer(1, 20))

story.append(Paragraph("<b>Purpose:</b> Define the exact process to verify cleaners and activate them for bookings.", styles["Normal"]))
story.append(Spacer(1, 12))

# Text diagram
diagram_text = """
CLEANER ONBOARDING DECISION FLOW

Cleaner Signup
     |
     v
[STRIPE IDENTITY — ID + SELFIE MATCH]
     |-- FAIL --> Retry Verification (Cleaner Action Required)
     |
     v
[CHECKR BACKGROUND CHECK]
     |-- FAIL/CONSIDER --> Admin Review & Reject
     |
     v
[INSURANCE UPLOAD]
     |-- INVALID/EXPIRED --> Request New Proof
     |
     v
[STRIPE CONNECT PAYOUT SETUP]
     |-- INCOMPLETE --> Cleaner Must Finish Banking Setup
     |
     v
 ✅ ALL CHECKS PASSED → Admin Activates Cleaner Profile
"""
story.append(Paragraph("<b>Verification Logic Diagram</b>", styles["Heading3"]))
story.append(Paragraph(diagram_text.replace("\n", "<br/>"), ParagraphStyle("mono", fontName="Courier", leading=12)))
story.append(PageBreak())

# Checklist
story.append(Paragraph("<b>Verification Checklist</b>", styles["Heading2"]))
table_data = [
    ["Step", "Requirement", "Admin Result"],
    ["1. Contact Verification", "Email + Phone Verified", "Pending / Verified"],
    ["2. Identity (Stripe)", "ID + Live Selfie Matches", "Pass / Fail / Pending"],
    ["3. Background Check (Checkr)", "Clear Background Check", "Clear / Consider / Fail"],
    ["4. Insurance", "Valid Insurance Uploaded + Approved", "Approved / Rejected"],
    ["5. Stripe Connect", "Banking + SSN Verified", "Active / Incomplete"],
    ["6. Activation", "All Checks Passed → Go Live", "Active / Pending"],
]
table = Table(table_data, colWidths=[120, 300, 100])
table.setStyle(TableStyle([
    ('GRID', (0,0), (-1,-1), 1, colors.black),
    ('BACKGROUND', (0,0), (-1,0), colors.lightgrey),
    ('VALIGN', (0,0), (-1,-1), 'MIDDLE'),
]))
story.append(table)
story.append(PageBreak())

# SOP Content
story.append(Paragraph("<b>ADMIN SOP — STEP-BY-STEP</b>", styles["Heading2"]))
bullet_style = styles["Bullet"]

steps = [
    "Navigate to Admin → Cleaners → Pending Verification.",
    "Open cleaner record → Verification Panel displays all checkpoints.",
    "Stripe Identity result updates automatically from webhook.",
    "Click 'Send Background Check' to trigger Checkr.",
    "Review insurance upload for: legal name match, active dates, and coverage.",
    "Verify Stripe Connect = ACTIVE (bank setup completed).",
    "If ALL checks are green → Click 'Activate Cleaner'.",
]
for step in steps:
    story.append(Paragraph(step, bullet_style))

story.append(Spacer(1, 20))
story.append(Paragraph("<b>Activation Rule:</b> A cleaner cannot accept jobs until ALL systems report VERIFIED.", styles["Normal"]))

doc.build(story)
file_path

✅ PURETASK OPERATIONS MANUAL
MODULE 1 — CLEANER VERIFICATION & COMPLIANCE (TEXT VERSION)
PURPOSE
This module defines the exact steps required to verify and activate a cleaner (Pro) on PureTask.
A Pro may not appear in search or accept bookings until they have passed all verification gates:

Identity Verified (Stripe Identity)

Background Check Clear (Checkr)

Insurance Valid and Approved

Stripe Connect Payouts Active

Email and Phone Verified

Only after all requirements are completed does the admin activate the Pro.

SECTION 1 — VERIFICATION DECISION LOGIC (NUMBERED FLOW)
(1) Identity Verification (Stripe Identity)
    - ID scan is completed
    - Selfie / liveness check matches the ID
    IF FAIL → cleaner retries verification
    IF PASS → move to Step 2

(2) Background Check (Checkr)
    - Consent captured
    - Webhook returns status: CLEAR / CONSIDER / FAIL
    IF FAIL or CONSIDER → admin reviews & blocks activation
    IF CLEAR → move to Step 3

(3) Insurance Upload / Documentation
    - Cleaner uploads proof of liability insurance
    - Admin verifies name, coverage, expiration date
    IF INVALID or EXPIRED → request new proof
    IF VALID → move to Step 4

(4) Stripe Connect — Payout Setup
    - Cleaner enters bank info & passes Stripe’s identity check
    - Stripe returns status ACTIVE
    IF INCOMPLETE → cleaner must finish onboarding
    IF ACTIVE → move to Step 5

(5) Activation Gate
    IF (1 + 2 + 3 + 4 + email + phone verified)
        → Admin sets status = ACTIVE
    ELSE
        → Keep status PENDING + show reason to cleaner
SECTION 2 — VERIFICATION CHECKLIST (ADMIN)

SECTION 3 — BASE44 ADMIN SOP (STEP-BY-STEP)
These are the exact clicks you make as the admin.

1. Go to: Admin Dashboard → Cleaners → Status = PENDING VERIFICATION

2. Open cleaner record.
   You will see the "Verification Panel" with 5 checkpoints.

3. ID Verification (Stripe Identity)
   - Check result: PASS / FAIL / PENDING
   - If FAIL → press "Request Re-Verification"

4. Background Check (Checkr)
   - Press "Send Background Check"
   - Wait for webhook to update status field

5. Insurance
   - Open uploaded file
   - Confirm: legal name, date valid, clear image
   - Click APPROVE or REJECT

6. Stripe Payout Setup
   - Check payout status: ACTIVE / NEEDS INFORMATION / INCOMPLETE
   - If incomplete → click "Resend Stripe Setup Link"

7. Activation
   - When all checkpoints are completed:
       Click → ACTIVATE CLEANER
   - Cleaner immediately appears in search + can accept bookings
ACTIVATION RULE (IMPORTANT)
A Pro becomes “ACTIVE” only when ALL systems say VERIFIED:

IF ID PASS
AND Background Check CLEAR
AND Insurance APPROVED
AND Stripe ACTIVE
AND Email/Phone Verified
THEN → Cleaner Status = ACTIVE
There should never be manual activation unless an override reason is added.

FAILURE HANDLING
ID FAIL → cleaner retries
BGC FAIL → cleaner blocked
INSURANCE FAIL → cleaner resubmits document
STRIPE INCOMPLETE → cleaner must finish banking setup
Every failure state gives the cleaner instructions on what to fix.

DATA / SECURITY RULES
Admin never downloads ID or stores images manually.

Stripe and Checkr maintain secure storage — PureTask stores status only.

Verification views are admin-only.

COMPLETION OUTCOME
Once active, cleaner receives:

“Your profile is live — you can now accept bookings.”

The reliability score begins once they complete their first job.

    ↓

    ↓

        - Checklist appears: tasks required + optional tasks
    ↓

        - Must match same areas as "Before" photos
    ↓

        ↓
        Job enters: CLIENT REVIEW PENDING

🎯 PURPOSE OF MODULE 4
This module defines:

How payments work (client → Stripe → PureTask → Cleaner)

✅ SECTION 1 — PAYMENT FLOW OVERVIEW (THE MONEY PATH)
CLIENT → STRIPE (payment hold) → PAYMENT CAPTURE → SPLIT PAYOUT

IF JOB APPROVED:
    Cleaner receives payout via Stripe Connect
    PureTask takes platform fee automatically
At booking (before job):
Card is authorized, not charged

Shows as “pending transaction” to client

Stripe PaymentIntent status = requires_capture

After job completion + photos approved:
PureTask triggers capture

Stripe splits funds:

Client payment → Stripe → (split)

   • Cleaner → Payout (Stripe Connect Express account)
   • Platform → Service fee deposited to PureTask Stripe account
✅ SECTION 2 — PLATFORM FEES (EXAMPLE MODEL)
Item	Amount
Platform fee	20% (deducted automatically)
Stripe processing fee	2.9% + 30¢
Instant payout (optional)	Cleaner pays extra 1.5%
Example: $150 cleaning job

Recipient	Amount
Cleaner receives	$118.05
PureTask revenue	$30.00
Stripe fee	$4.35

✅ SECTION 4 — DISPUTE MANAGEMENT SYSTEM
When a client reports an issue:
Client → "Report Issue" button → Uploads photos + text description
   |
   v
System tags job as: DISPUTE_OPEN
   |
   v
Cleaner receives notification: "Client requested changes"
   |
   v
Cleaner must respond within 24 hours
Admin sees:

Before vs. After photos

Client’s submitted issue

Cleaner response

Chat thread evidence

ADMIN DECISION TREE
IF cleaner agrees to return → job REOPENED until completion
IF cleaner refuses → issue credit to client / partial payout
IF proof favors cleaner → release payout immediately
DISPUTE OUTCOMES
Outcome	Result
Cleaner resolves issue	Full payout
Client still unsatisfied	Partial payout or credit
Cleaner shows strong proof	Full payout to cleaner
Cleaner ghost / no response	No payout + score penalty
✅ SECTION 5 — BACKUP CLEANER ESCALATION
If the selected cleaner doesn't accept the job within timeframe:

(1) System waits 4 hours (or shorter depending on config)
(2) If no response → automatically offers job to next "favorited" cleaner
(3) Cleaner #2 gets request
(4) If still no response → Cleaner #3
(5) If no one accepts → alert Admin to intervene
Admin sees:

💡 “This job is unassigned — select a cleaner manually or refund.”

✅ MODULE 7 — DAILY OPERATIONS, ADMIN WORKFLOWS & SUPPORT PLAYBOOK
PURETASK OPERATIONS MANUAL — EXTREME DETAIL VERSION
(Words only — copy/paste into Notion / PDF later)

🎯 PURPOSE OF MODULE 7
This module defines the complete daily management system of PureTask:

Admin responsibilities (daily / weekly / monthly)

What to do when jobs come in

How to monitor cleaner reliability

How to handle disputes, refunds, chargebacks

System alerts / automations

KPIs you track to ensure growth

After this module, anyone should be able to run PureTask operations even if you're not there.

✅ SECTION 1 — DAILY OPERATIONS CHECKLIST (Admin)
EVERY DAY (15–30 minutes)

1. Check bookings
    [ ] Pending cleaner responses
    [ ] Any jobs stuck without a cleaner
    [ ] Escalate to backup cleaners if needed

2. Check disputes
    [ ] New customer complaints
    [ ] Photo review → approve or deny dispute

3. Check payouts
    [ ] All completed jobs processed
    [ ] Any payout held or delayed

4. Cleaner onboarding
    [ ] ID verification
    [ ] Insurance doc approval
    [ ] Background check review
    [ ] Stripe payout setup status

5. Support inbox
    [ ] Client messages
    [ ] Cleaner questions
    [ ] FAQ responses

6. Metric snapshots
    [ ] # of bookings today
    [ ] # of active cleaners
    [ ] Reliability score low warnings
✅ SECTION 2 — WEEKLY OPERATIONS (Admin)
EVERY FRIDAY (30–60 minutes)

1. Check reliability score dashboard
   [ ] Flag any cleaner below 67 (Tier 1 — Risk)
   [ ] Offer coaching or removal

2. Review cleaner performance
   [ ] Completion rate (finish jobs?)
   [ ] Acceptance rate (say yes to jobs?)

3. Review support trends
   [ ] Top complaints
   [ ] Most common disputes

4. Review growth metrics
   [ ] New cleaners onboarded
   [ ] New client bookings
   [ ] Revenue generated
✅ SECTION 3 — MONTHLY OPERATIONS
EVERY MONTH (60–90 minutes)

1. Stripe → download monthly reports
2. Export cleaned-up data to finance tool (Notion or Quickbooks)
3. Send feedback survey to cleaners
4. Send “reactivation” promotions to inactive clients
✅ SECTION 4 — PURETASK PRIORITY SYSTEM
Only 3 things matter operationally:

Priority	Goal
#1	Keep jobs staffed (supply + demand balance)
#2	Keep reliability score accurate
#3	Keep Stripe payouts flowing cleanly
Everything else is optional.

✅ SECTION 5 — JOB LIFECYCLE (operations POV)
(1) CLIENT REQUESTS JOB
    ↓
(2) CLEANER ACCEPTS (or backup cleaner auto assigned)
    ↓
(3) CLEANER ARRIVES (GPS Check-In)
    ↓
(4) BEFORE PHOTOS → checklist → AFTER PHOTOS
    ↓
(5) CLIENT APPROVES
    ↓
(6) STRIPE PAYMENT CAPTURED
    ↓
(7) PAYOUT RELEASED TO CLEANER
Admin monitors steps 2, 4, and 7.

✅ SECTION 6 — ADMIN SOP (step-by-step)
📌 When a job comes in (new booking)
→ Check if a cleaner accepted within 4 hours.
→ If not, click "Assign Backup Cleaner".
→ If no backup cleaners available, message client.
📌 When a cleaner submits photos
→ Review before + after images
→ If something missing, reopen job
→ If good, approve → triggers Stripe capture
📌 When client disputes
Admin → Dispute Portal

Step 1: Ask cleaner for explanation
Step 2: Compare before/after
Step 3: Decide outcome:
    - Cleaner redo job
    - Partial credit
    - Full refund
Step 4: Update booking status
Step 5: Notify both sides
Dispute outcomes are logged in cleaner performance history.

✅ SECTION 7 — RELIABILITY SCORE RESPONSE RULES
Score Range	Tier	Action
90–100	Elite	Promote to VIP cleaners list
78–89	Trusted	Maintain
67–77	Reliable	Monitor, coach
0–66	Risk	Temporary removal until improvement
Admin only intervenes at 67 or below.

✅ SECTION 8 — SUPPORT AUTOMATION (short replies)
Client asks “When will cleaner arrive?”
The cleaner checks in via GPS when they arrive at your address, and you will see it live from your dashboard.

Cleaner asks “When will I get paid?”
After you upload after-photos and the client approves, we trigger payout via Stripe.
Standard payout: 1–2 business days
Instant payout (optional): available for 1.5% fee

Client wants a refund
Refunds are based on our Happiness Guarantee — if the work doesn’t match the agreed checklist, we send cleaner back or issue credit.

✅ SECTION 9 — KPIs AND DASHBOARDS
These should appear on PlatformMetrics.jsx dashboard (already in your project files):

KPI	Target
Booking acceptance rate	> 70%
Cleaner reliability average	> 85
Disputes per 100 jobs	< 5%
Repeat booking rate	> 40%
✅ SECTION 10 — ADMIN ESCALATION FLOW
Cleaner misses job → -25 score → notify → temp removal (if repeated)
Client disputes → Job on hold → investigate → payout decision
No cleaners accept job → Admin assigns cleaner manually
Cleaners that cause repeated disputes are let go.

# 🚀 Daily Operations Checklist

👤 Admin Name: ___________
📅 Date: ___________

---

## 🔁 MORNING ROUTINE (15 minutes)

[ ] Check **Bookings Screen** in Base44
      → Any stuck on "Pending Cleaner Response"
      → If yes, assign Backup Cleaner

[ ] Check **Disputes**
      → Jobs flagged as "Client requests changes"
      → Review photos and cleaner notes

[ ] Check **Payout Queue**
      → After photos approved → payout should be queued

---

## 📥 New Cleaner Applications

[ ] ID verified (Checkr / Stripe)
[ ] Background passed
[ ] Insurance uploaded
[ ] Payout setup completed (Stripe)

---

## 📊 Reliability Alerts

[ ] Look at Reliability dashboard
      → Any cleaner below **67 score**
      → Flag them & send improvement script

---

## 📦 Support Inbox

[ ] Client messages (respond within 12 hours)
[ ] Cleaner messages (respond within 12 hours)

---

## END-OF-DAY

[ ] All payouts released (unless dispute)
[ ] Pending bookings escalated to backups
[ ] Tasks documented in Notion

✅ PAGE 3 — 🛠 TROUBLESHOOTING PLAYBOOK
If something breaks → check this first.

✅ TEMPLATE
# 🛠 Troubleshooting Playbook

---

## 🚫 Booking stuck on "Pending Cleaner Response"

CAUSE:
Cleaner did not respond within 4 hours.

FIX:
1. Assign Backup Cleaner
2. Notify client: “Finding a new Cleaner”

---

## 🚫 Client says: "Cleaner never showed up"

CHECK:
[ ] Did GPS check-in happen?

FIX:
→ No GPS check-in = no payout.
→ Assign backup cleaner ASAP.

---

## 🚫 Cleaner says: "I can't complete booking — can't upload photos"

FIX:
→ Ask cleaner to:
   - Restart app
   - Switch to wifi
→ If still broken: Admin uploads for them.

---

## 🚫 Client disputes “missed tasks”

FIX:
1. Compare before vs. after photos
2. If task missing → open job for redo
3. If cleaner refuses → partial refund to client
4. Score penalty = -10 to cleaner

---

## 🚫 Stripe payout didn't go through

CHECK:
[ ] Stripe Connect status = Verified?
[ ] Bank account validated?
[ ] Payout on hold due to dispute?

FIX:
→ Hit “Resend Stripe onboarding link”

🚨 Troubleshooting Playbook — PureTask Operations

I’m going to build 5 master decision trees:

Cleaner does not respond to booking request

Cleaner no-show on job day

Client disputes the cleaning (not happy with results)

Payment fails (Stripe hold / capture declined)

Each tree includes:

What triggers it

Admin actions in Base44 / Stripe

What communication to send to client + cleaner

When to update score / log event

✅ Decision Tree #1 — CLEANER DOES NOT RESPOND TO BOOKING REQUEST
📌 Trigger:
Client books → Cleaner does not accept within 4 hours.
                Booking Request Sent
                          ↓
            Has the cleaner responded?
                     /         \
                  YES           NO
                 /              \
        → They accept        After 4 hours?
                              /        \
                           NO          YES
                           |           |
                      Send automated     ↓
                      reminder           ↓
                                    Is backup cleaner
                                      available?
                                    /            \
                                 YES              NO
                                 |                 |
           Auto-assign backup cleaner         Notify client +
              (2nd or 3rd favorite)             offer to:
                   ↓                            • Keep job open 12 hrs
        Notify client + cleaner                   • Request quotes instead
                   ↓
         Score Log: +1 for responsiveness
✅ Reliability automation rules:

If cleaner accepts within 4 hours → +2 score

If cleaner ignores request → ‐3 score

If admin has to assign backup → ‐5 score

✅ Decision Tree #2 — CLEANER NO-SHOW
📌 Trigger:
Job marked "In Progress" but no GPS check-in after start time + 30 minutes.
                        Start Time Reached
                               ↓
                      GPS Check-In Completed?
                           /         \
                        YES           NO
                        |             |
             → Normal job flow        ↓
                              30 min grace passed?
                                     /       \
                                   NO        YES
                                             ↓
                                  Attempt 1 - SMS Notify
                                             ↓
                        Did cleaner reply within 10 min?
                                  /         \
                                YES          NO
                                |            |
                     Reschedule or ETA OK     ↓
                                       Attempt 2 - Call cleaner
                                              ↓
                            Still no response?
                                 /            \
                               YES             NO
                               ↓                |
                   Mark as NO-SHOW             ETA accepted
                               ↓
                   Auto-assign backup cleaner
                               ↓
                        Score penalty -25
                               ↓
              Auto-refund authorization to client
✅ Decision Tree #3 — CLIENT DISPUTE (Not satisfied with cleaning)
📌 Trigger:
Client selects "Request Review" instead of "Approve Photos"
                      Client opens dispute
                               ↓
               Create DISPUTE record in Notion DB
                               ↓
                   Lock payout in Stripe (no release)
                               ↓
                      Review photo gallery
                         /           \
                Photos missing?    Photos valid?
                     /               \
                  YES                 NO
                  |                   |
      Request cleaner to return      ↓
         within 48 hours             ↓
        Score: -10 (poor proof)   Ask client:
                     ↓           "What exactly was missed?"
                     ↓                   ↓
         Cleaner returns?        Is client still unhappy?
            /        \                  /         \
          YES         NO            YES           NO
          |           |             |             |
   Client signs        Refund partial        Release payout
   approval            OR full refund        Score cleaner +5
Refund logic:

If cleaner refuses to return → full refund, score -25

If cleaner returns + client approves → score +3

✅ Decision Tree #4 — PAYMENT FAILED (Stripe)
📌 Trigger:
Stripe authorization fails or card declines at final capture
                 Payment Fails
                      ↓
           Is it an AUTHORIZED hold?
                 /            \
               YES             NO
               |               |
  Notify client to update      ↓
       payment method      Hard decline?
               |               /     \
      Allow 24 hours         YES      NO (bank error)
          to fix               |         |
               ↓        Cancel booking    \
       Payment method updated?            Retry in 30 minutes
            /        \
          YES        NO
          |           |
   Resume booking    Auto-cancel + notify client
Score impact: none — payment issues are not the cleaner’s fault

✅ Decision Tree #5 — DAMAGE / INSURANCE CLAIM
📌 Trigger:
Client reports damage OR cleaner reports injury while on site.
                  Damage Report Submitted
                              ↓
                  Collect evidence (photos)
                              ↓
                 Is cleaner insured (verified)?
                          /           \
                        YES           NO
                        |              |
         File through cleaner’s insurance   ↓
                    |                       ↓
              PureTask discretionary payout   ↓
                       ↓                  Score -30
             Close claim & notify client

Great question — here’s the difference in the simplest possible explanation:

✅ PRIVATE KNOWLEDGE BASE (Internal Only — Admin / You / Staff)
Who can see it:
Only you and anyone on your internal PureTask team.

What goes in it:

Internal scripts (how to talk to a client during dispute)

Score penalty rules

Verification procedures

Background check SOP

How to remove a problem cleaner

How to override payment / refunds

Admin-only troubleshooting

Why choose PRIVATE:

Keeps operational tactics confidential

Cleaners/clients don’t see internal scoring rules

Prevents system gaming (“if I do X I won't lose points”)

Allows candid notes (“avoid this cleaner, they cause problems”)

Analogy:
Like the manager handbook at a restaurant — workers don't see the escalation policies.

✅ PUBLIC KNOWLEDGE BASE (Viewed by Clients + Cleaners)
Who can see it:

Anyone using PureTask (clients + cleaners)

What goes in it:

Common FAQs (“How do I book?”)

Expectations (“Cleaner will send before/after photos”)

How check-in works (GPS check-in)

Cancellation / reschedule policy

How cleaners get paid

Uploading insurance or ID instructions

Why choose PUBLIC:

Reduces support messages

Builds trust

Educates clients before they book

Analogy:
Like Uber Help Center — riders and drivers both see it.

🔥 WHICH SHOULD YOU PICK FOR PURETASK?
✅ BEST STRATEGY FOR MARKETPLACES (Uber, DoorDash, Thumbtack)

Type	Who sees it	Purpose
PUBLIC	Clients + Cleaners	Education + reduce support
PRIVATE	You + Admin team	SOPs + decision trees + scoring rules

but the CONTROL to be private.

Public KB: “Photos are required to complete the job.”

Private KB: “If photos aren’t submitted → score -10 and hold payout.”

✅ PAGE 6A — PUBLIC KNOWLEDGE BASE
(Paste into a new Notion page)

Page name:

🌐 PureTask Help Center (Public)
📚 CLEANER FAQ
(Add as toggles)

➤ How do I get paid?

Payments are processed through Stripe. Payouts are released after the client approves the before/after photos.

➤ Do I need insurance?

Yes. Proof of liability insurance is required to unlock the “Verified Pro” badge.

➤ What if a client cancels?

If canceled more than 24 hours before the job → no penalty.
If canceled same-day → cleaner receives a 25% cancellation fee.

➤ What happens if I forget to check in?

Jobs require GPS check-in and before/after photos to release payment.

📚 CLIENT FAQ
➤ When am I charged?

Your card is authorized at booking, but not charged until:

Cleaner finishes the job

Photos are submitted

You approve the job

➤ What if I’m not happy?

Tap: “Request Review” → Upload photos → Explain concern
Your payment is paused until resolved.

➤ Can I talk to the cleaner before booking?

Yes — messaging unlocks once you start a booking request.

🧾 POLICIES (Public)
Policy	Rules
Photos Required	Cleaner must submit before & after photos
GPS Check-in	Required to confirm arrival
Rescheduling	>24 hours: free / <24 hours: cleaner may charge
💰 Money + Payouts
Stage	Status
Booking submitted	Card authorized
Cleaner completes + uploads photos	Job pending approval
Client approves	Payment captured + payout released

→ PureTask auto-assigns a backup Pro.

→ Yes, messaging unlocks after request is sent.

→ Photos + notes are reviewed. Cleaner can return within 48 hours.

What if I don't know what to select (standard vs deep clean)?
→ Use Quick Book. We auto-select based on home size.

✅ First — Are the current scripts long enough?
TikTok ideal VO length:

6–12 seconds for short viral meme content

12–22 seconds for ads or booking-focused sales videos

Anything over 25 seconds loses engagement unless it's storytelling

Your current scripts are:

Script category	Avg length	Suitable?	Notes
Client Booking (1–5)	~7–10 seconds	✅ Good, but could benefit from 2–3 extra lines for ad versions	
Meme/Funny (6–10)	~4–7 seconds	✅ Perfect for short humor videos	
So the meme ones are short on purpose — that’s ideal.

But the client booking scripts probably need to be longer if:

We want to use them as ads

You plan to have B-roll transitions, screen recordings, etc.

Right now, they are sized correctly for quick-scroll TikToks, but not ad-level storytelling videos.

ok so i have some questions . do  i have to have a seperate schedualing system for puretask or does base 44 handle that, becuase it seems like base 44 might keep goood records but does not actually send  out notifications or am i wrong?

Great question — and you're not crazy.
This is the exact confusion most Base44 builders run into.

✅ Short Answer
Base44 stores data and runs logic,
but Base44 does NOT automatically handle scheduling or send notifications unless you set up automation or integrations.

So yes:

Base44 → database + UI + workflows

Scheduling and notifications → require automation

Usually with:

n8n (built-in to Base44)

or Zapier / Make.com

and third-party services like Twilio (SMS), SendGrid (email), or Push notifications.

✅ Breakdown
What Base44 does well:
Capability	Base44 handles it?
Saves booking date/time	✅ Yes
Stores cleaner + client details	✅ Yes
Tracks job status (requested, accepted, completed)	✅ Yes
Calculates reliability score	✅ Yes
Generates UI (dashboards, modals, tables)	✅ Yes
What Base44 does NOT do automatically:
Need	Base44 built-in?	Requires
Send SMS reminders to cleaner	❌	Twilio + automation (n8n / workflow)
Send mobile push notifications	❌	Push service integration
Email notifications (booking confirmed, job reminder)	⚠️ Manual	SendGrid / SMTP setup
Auto-reschedule if not accepted	❌	Workflow logic (conditions + cron)
Recurring scheduling / auto-jobs	❌	Cron automation
✅ How scheduling workflow should be set up
[ Client selects date/time ]
           ↓
[ Base44 stores booking in database ]
           ↓
[ n8n scheduled workflow triggers reminders ]
           ↓
[ SMS/Push sent to cleaner + client ]
           ↓
[ Cleaner accepts or declines ]
           ↓
[ If no response in 4 hours → backup cleaner notified ]
You already have JobStartRemindersCron.jsx in your code files (I saw it when you uploaded your project).
That component checks for upcoming jobs, but it still requires an automation to actually send notifications.

✅ What you need to add
Minimal setup (recommended)
Tool	Purpose
Twilio	Send SMS
SendGrid	Send emails
n8n automations	Connect events → send notifications
Example Automation (n8n)
Trigger: Booking is created
Action: Send SMS to cleaner
If no response → reassign or send to backup cleaner

You don't need a "separate scheduling system."

You need:

Base44 = data + workflow logic

n8n = brain that triggers actions

Twilio / SendGrid = notification delivery

🚀 Final Answer
🎯 Base44 does NOT automatically send reminders or scheduling notifications.

You must integrate:

Twilio (SMS),

SendGrid (email),

and/or Push notifications via Expo or OneSignal.

You do NOT need a separate scheduling platform —
just automation that reacts to Base44 job data.

is there any service or platform that handles everything i need ?

✅ Direct Answer
No single platform does everything PureTask needs out-of-the-box.
You will always need a combination of:
platform (database + auth + UI) + automation + notification service.

BUT…

There are platforms that handle 90–95% of what you need, with far less custom wiring than Base44.

🔥 Here are the real options (ranked)
✅ Best All-In-One for Marketplaces (your use-case)
➤ Uppointment / TidyCal (Booking platform)
⭐ Handles: scheduling, reminders, calendar sync, SMS, rescheduling
❌ Does NOT handle: background check verification, reliability score, cleaner marketplace behavior
❌ Does NOT handle: “Proof Before Payment” workflows

➤ Jobber (built for home service companies)
✅ Scheduling
✅ Client reminders
✅ SMS + Email notifications
✅ Mobile app
✅ Payments
❌ Does NOT handle: marketplace multi-cleaner environment
❌ Cleaners cannot “claim” jobs (you assign them)

➤ HouseCall Pro (closest to Uber for cleaning)
✅ Scheduling
✅ Automated SMS reminders
✅ Cleaner mobile app
✅ Automated follow-ups + reviews
✅ Payments
❌ Doesn’t support independent contractors bidding / claiming jobs
❌ No reliability scoring / rating automation logic

✅ Handles contractor management
✅ Payouts to cleaners
✅ Clients can submit requests
✅ Internal messaging
❌ No cleaning marketplace logic
❌ Limited scheduling + automations

✅ Best No-Code Marketplace Builder (what you are building)
➤ Base44 + n8n + Twilio + Stripe Connect
👉 This is the only combination that gives you:

Feature	Supported?
Cleaners are independent contractors	✅
Background check verification	✅ (Checkr API)

“Approve photos before payment” workflow	✅

Job request → cleaner accepts → backup cleaner gets it	✅
This is why Uber-style apps are not built on single “all-in-one” platforms.

Because your needs are not “appointment booking”…

Your needs are marketplace orchestration + automation logic.

No real automation logic

Still need n8n / Twilio for scheduling reminders

✅ Reality: You’re building something unique

1) Automations Blueprint (n8n)
Or Zapier/Make equivalents—n8n is ideal because you already use Base44.

1.1 Booking → Cleaner Notification → Escalation
Trigger: New Booking created (status=REQUESTED)
Data needs in booking record:

booking_id

client_id

preferred_cleaner_id

backup_cleaner_ids (array of 1–3)

start_time, duration_hours

address, geo_lat, geo_lng

price_authorized (Stripe PI id)

status (REQUESTED → ACCEPTED → SCHEDULED → IN_PROGRESS → COMPLETED → CLIENT_REVIEW → APPROVED → PAID)

Workflow (n8n nodes):

Webhook/Interval Trigger: onCreate(booking) from Base44

HTTP Node → SMS (Twilio):
Send to preferred_cleaner_id:
“New job on [date/time] at [area]. Pay est: $[X]. Reply YES to accept or NO to pass.”

Wait Node (4h or configurable):
If status !== ACCEPTED, branch:

If NO / no response: iterate backup_cleaner_ids (for each: notify, wait 90m)

If any accepts → set status=ACCEPTED, assign accepted_cleaner_id, schedule reminders

Acceptance capture options:

SMS reply parsing via Twilio webhook → n8n → Base44 update

In-app accept button → Base44 API → n8n notifies others to stop

Nudge: 2h after first SMS, send: “Reminder: job starts [relative time]. Reply YES to accept.”

1.2 Pre-Job Reminders & GPS Check-in Enforcement
When status=ACCEPTED:

T-24h: SMS to client: “Reminder: [CleanerName] arrives tomorrow at [time].”

T-12h: SMS to cleaner: “You’re booked for [time], tap to view route [link].”

T-60m: SMS to both (arrival window)

T-0: Open GPS check-in window (±30 minutes).
n8n cron checks now between start_time ± 30m and sends:

To cleaner: “Please Check-In in the app. Failure after 30m flags no-show.”

If not checked in at +30m: mark risk_flag: NO_SHOW_WINDOW_EXCEEDED and notify admin + client.

1.3 Photo Proof & Client Approval → Payment Capture
When cleaner taps “Complete” (uploads photos):

Base44 sets status=COMPLETED, stores photos_before, photos_after, notes

n8n sends client email/SMS:
“Review photos & approve payment: [link]”

Auto-escalation: If no approval in 24h:

Reminder to client

Optional auto-approve after 48h if no dispute and photos present (policy choice)

On Client Approval:

n8n → Stripe: capture PaymentIntent

Set status=APPROVED

n8n → Stripe Connect transfer to cleaner (if stripe_connect_status=enabled)

Mark status=PAID, store payout_transfer_id

1.4 Disputes + Make-Good Loop
Trigger: Client taps “Open Dispute”

n8n pauses payout (do not capture PI)

Request evidence via form (attach photos/notes)

Offer “Return Visit” option to cleaner (48h to complete)

Outcomes:

Cleaner fixes & client approves: capture PI → small +Reliability (+3)

Cleaner refuses/no-show: refund client → Reliability penalties (-25)

Partial credit: capture partial → issue credit via Stripe/ledger

1.5 Reliability Score Automation (you already have code)
UpdateReliabilityScores.jsx runs nightly or per-event. Tie events to points:

On-time check-in: +2

Job completed with approval: +3

No-show: -25

Late check-in (>30m): -5

Dispute opened: -10 (recovered: +3)

n8n can POST to your internal endpoint to recalc after each event.

1.6 Recurring Jobs
RecurringBookingGenerator.jsx runs weekly:

For each recurring contract create next occurrence 14–21 days out

Auto-notify cleaner 48h in advance to confirm

If cleaner declines, fire BackupCleanerFinder.jsx

2) Twilio Integration (SMS)
Minimal, reliable, scalable. You can add email (SendGrid) and push (OneSignal/Expo) later.

2.1 What you need
Twilio account (+ SMS-enabled number)

n8n HTTP Request nodes to Twilio API

One Inbound SMS webhook in Twilio → n8n for reply parsing (YES/NO/HELP)

Outbound SMS sample (n8n HTTP node):

POST https://api.twilio.com/2010-04-01/Accounts/{ACCOUNT_SID}/Messages.json
Auth: Basic (ACCOUNT_SID:AUTH_TOKEN)
Body:
  To=+1XXXXXXXXXX
  From=+1YYYYYYYYYY
  Body="New job [date/time], [area], est $[x]. Reply YES to accept, NO to pass."
Inbound SMS → n8n Webhook → Router:

If body contains YES:

Update Booking: status=ACCEPTED, accepted_cleaner_id

Notify client: “Confirmed”

Cancel any pending fallback timers

If body contains NO:

Trigger next backup cleaner notification

Else:

Send help text

Templates to pre-write (admin-editable text):

New job request

Reminders (24h, 12h, 60m)

Check-in prompt

Photo approval request

Dispute acknowledgment

Payout confirmation

Store templates in Base44 so you can edit copy without touching flows.

2.2 Optional: Email + Push
Email (SendGrid/SMTP) for long-form messages (approval links, receipts)

Push (OneSignal/Expo) for in-app prompts; needs mobile app or PWA service worker

3) Visual System Flow (Text Diagram)
CLIENT books → Booking(REQUESTED) saved in Base44
        └─n8n→ SMS to Preferred Cleaner (YES/NO)
                    └─YES→ set ACCEPTED, assign cleaner
                    └─NO / 4h elapsed→ notify Backup #1 → Backup #2 → ...
ACCEPTED → schedule reminders (24h/12h/60m) to client + cleaner
T-0 → GPS Check-In window (±30m)
      └ if no check-in at +30m → flag NO_SHOW_WINDOW_EXCEEDED → admin alert
Cleaner completes + uploads photos → status=COMPLETED
        └─n8n→ request Client Approval via link
                └ APPROVED→ Stripe capture → Connect payout → status=PAID
                └ DISPUTE→ pause capture → offer Return Visit (48h)
                      └ fixed+approved → capture + small +score
                      └ refused → refund client + score penalty
Nightly → Reliability recalculation (events → points → tier)
Recurring → Generate next job → notify cleaner → accept/decline → fallback if needed
4) Data Model (fields to add/confirm)
Booking

booking_id

client_id, accepted_cleaner_id

preferred_cleaner_id, backup_cleaner_ids (array)

start_time, duration_hours

address, geo_lat, geo_lng

status

photos_before[], photos_after[]

payment_intent_id, connect_account_id, payout_transfer_id

risk_flag (enum: NO_SHOW_WINDOW_EXCEEDED, etc.)

approval_deadline (timestamp, for 24–48h auto-approve)

Cleaner

phone_verified, email_verified, bg_check_status, insurance_verified

stripe_connect_status

reliability_score, reliability_tier

last_check_in_at, no_show_count

Client

phone_verified, email_verified, address_verified

preferred_products (optional)

5) SOPs & Checks (copy into Notion)

☐ Review “Today’s Jobs” (check-ins within window)

☐ Approvals pending >24h (send reminders)

☐ Disputes open >48h (resolve or refund)

☐ Stripe transfers pending (payouts)

Weekly

☐ Reliability anomalies (big drops)

☐ Recurring jobs generated

☐ Template copy QA (SMS/email)

☐ Backup cleaner coverage saturation (supply)

6) n8n Flow Starters (Node Outlines)
Flow A: On Booking Created

Trigger: Webhook POST /n8n/booking-created

Node: Get Booking Details

Node: Twilio SMS → Preferred Cleaner

Node: Wait 4h

IF status!=ACCEPTED → ForEach backup list:

SMS → Wait 90m → IF accepted break

Flow B: Reminders

Cron: every 5 min

Node: query bookings starting within 24h/12h/60m

Node: send corresponding SMS/email

Node: write reminder_sent_* flags to Booking

Flow C: Check-in Watch

Cron: every 5 min

Node: query ACCEPTED bookings in window

Node: if no check-in and >30m → set flag, notify admin/client

Flow D: Approval & Payout

Trigger: status=COMPLETED (webhook)

Node: send approval link to client

Wait: 24h (reminder), 48h (auto-approve optional)

On approval: Stripe capture → Connect transfer → set PAID

Flow E: Dispute Handling

Trigger: Dispute created

Node: pause capture

Node: request evidence

Node: offer return visit to cleaner

Branch: fix vs refund → update reliability score via internal endpoint

7) Twilio Message Examples (ready to paste)
New Job → Cleaner

“PureTask: New job [DATE TIME], [AREA]. Est $[X], [HOURS]h. Reply YES to accept, NO to pass.”

Client → Confirmation

“PureTask: Your request is sent to [CleanerName]. You’ll be notified when they accept.”

Reminder (12h) → Cleaner

“Reminder: [JOB TIME] tomorrow. Tap for route: [shortlink].”

Check-In Prompt

“You can now Check-In for [JOB TIME] at [ADDRESS]. Please confirm within 30 min.”

Approval Request

“Review your cleaner’s photos & approve payment: [link]”

Dispute Acknowledged

“We’re on it. We’ve notified your cleaner to return within 48 hours.”

8) Stripe Connect Notes (critical)
Collect cleaner KYC (Stripe-hosted onboarding link)

Block payouts if connect_account.status != enabled

Always authorize at booking, capture after approval

Save payment_intent_id on booking

9) Security & Compliance
Mask client address in SMS (show area, not full address)

Avoid sending links with PII; use secure tokens

Log all SMS and state changes in an audit table

Respect opt-out (“STOP”) for SMS through Twilio

# Create SVG logo assets and a brand guide PDF, then zip everything for download.
import os, zipfile, io, textwrap
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import LETTER
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
from reportlab.lib.units import inch

base_dir = "/mnt/data/PureTask_LogoAssets"
os.makedirs(base_dir, exist_ok=True)

# Brand colors
ROYAL_BLUE = "#005CFF"
AQUA = "#2FE7D6"
GOLD = "#F9C74F"
WHITE = "#FFFFFF"
NAVY = "#0A162A"

# Simple SVG templates for three "P" styles
def svg_header(w, h):
    return f'<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="{w}" height="{h}" viewBox="0 0 {w} {h}">'

def svg_footer():
    return '</svg>'

def gradient_def(id_="grad1", start=ROYAL_BLUE, end=AQUA):
    return f'''
    <defs>
      <linearGradient id="{id_}" x1="0" y1="0" x2="1" y2="1">
        <stop offset="0%" stop-color="{start}"/>
        <stop offset="100%" stop-color="{end}"/>
      </linearGradient>
    </defs>
    '''

# P icon geometries (simple and clean)
def p_icon_rounded(fill="url(#grad1)"):
    # rounded "P" using a circle + rounded rectangle (donut style)
    return f'''
    {gradient_def() if "url(" in fill else ""}
    <g transform="translate(128,64)">
      <!-- stem -->
      <rect x="0" y="0" width="96" height="320" rx="48" ry="48" fill="{fill}"/>
      <!-- bowl -->
      <path d="M96,0 h128 a96,96 0 0 1 0,192 h-128 z" fill="{fill}"/>
      <!-- inner knockout (white) to make P counter) -->
      <path d="M128,48 h80 a48,48 0 0 1 0,96 h-80 z" fill="{WHITE}"/>
    </g>
    '''

def p_icon_geometric(fill="url(#grad1)"):
    # geometric "P" with sharp corners
    return f'''
    {gradient_def() if "url(" in fill else ""}
    <g transform="translate(128,64)">
      <rect x="0" y="0" width="80" height="320" fill="{fill}"/>
      <rect x="80" y="0" width="160" height="120" fill="{fill}"/>
      <rect x="80" y="120" width="80" height="80" fill="{WHITE}"/>
    </g>
    '''

def p_icon_split(fill="url(#grad1)"):
    # split-stroke premium "P": two shapes with a diagonal cut
    return f'''
    {gradient_def() if "url(" in fill else ""}
    <g transform="translate(128,64)">
      <!-- left stem -->
      <rect x="0" y="0" width="64" height="320" rx="24" ry="24" fill="{fill}"/>
      <!-- outer bowl -->
      <path d="M64,0 h144 a96,96 0 0 1 0,192 h-144 z" fill="{fill}"/>
      <!-- diagonal split knockout -->
      <path d="M64,40 L224,0 L224,60 L64,100 Z" fill="{WHITE}" opacity="0.95"/>
      <!-- inner bowl knockout -->
      <path d="M96,56 h88 a48,48 0 0 1 0,96 h-88 z" fill="{WHITE}"/>
    </g>
    '''

def make_svg(icon_fn, filename, w=512, h=512, fill="url(#grad1)"):
    svg = svg_header(w,h) + icon_fn(fill=fill) + svg_footer()
    with open(os.path.join(base_dir, filename), "w") as f:
        f.write(svg)

# Create flat and gradient SVGs for each style
styles = [
    ("rounded", p_icon_rounded),
    ("geometric", p_icon_geometric),
    ("split", p_icon_split),
]

for name, fn in styles:
    # gradient
    make_svg(fn, f"p_{name}_gradient.svg", fill="url(#grad1)")
    # flat blue
    make_svg(fn, f"p_{name}_flat_blue.svg", fill=ROYAL_BLUE)
    # flat aqua
    make_svg(fn, f"p_{name}_flat_aqua.svg", fill=AQUA)

# Create wordmark lockups as simple SVGs (icon + text)
def make_lockup(icon_svg_filename, out_filename, text="PureTask", color=ROYAL_BLUE, gradient=True):
    # simple lockup: embed icon via <image> isn't ideal, so re-use path by reading the icon file
    with open(os.path.join(base_dir, icon_svg_filename), "r") as f:
        icon_svg = f.read()
    # Extract inner <g> block
    inner = icon_svg.split(">",1)[1].rsplit("<",1)[0]  # crude extraction between first and last tags
    # Build lockup svg
    w,h = 900, 300
    svg = [svg_header(w,h)]
    if gradient and 'linearGradient' in icon_svg:
        # re-add gradient definition
        svg.append(gradient_def())
    # Place icon
    svg.append('<g transform="translate(20, -10) scale(0.45)">' + inner + "</g>")
    # Wordmark text (rounded-ish look via font-family stack; true font embedding omitted)
    svg.append(f'<text x="280" y="180" font-family="Nunito, Poppins, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif" font-weight="700" font-size="120" fill="{color}">{text}</text>')
    svg.append(svg_footer())
    with open(os.path.join(base_dir, out_filename), "w") as f:
        f.write("".join(svg))

# Generate lockups (gradient + flat blue) for each style
for name, _ in styles:
    make_lockup(f"p_{name}_gradient.svg", f"lockup_{name}_gradient.svg", color=ROYAL_BLUE, gradient=True)
    make_lockup(f"p_{name}_flat_blue.svg", f"lockup_{name}_flat_blue.svg", color=ROYAL_BLUE, gradient=False)

# Create simple white background app icon PNG (rounded style as primary)
from PIL import Image, ImageDraw

def draw_primary_p_icon(img_size=1024, stroke=False, gradient=True):
    img = Image.new("RGBA", (img_size, img_size), (255,255,255,255))
    draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
    # We'll draw a simplified rounded P with flat royal blue (for PNG)
    # Stem
    stem_x, stem_y, stem_w, stem_h, r = 360, 210, 180, 620, 80
    draw.rounded_rectangle((stem_x, stem_y, stem_x+stem_w, stem_y+stem_h), r, fill=(0,92,255,255))
    # Bowl
    # outer
    bowl_rect = (stem_x+180, 210, stem_x+180+260, 210+200)
    draw.rounded_rectangle(bowl_rect, 90, fill=(0,92,255,255))
    # inner knockout (white)
    inner_rect = (stem_x+220, 250, stem_x+220+180, 250+120)
    draw.rounded_rectangle(inner_rect, 60, fill=(255,255,255,255))
    return img

app_dir = os.path.join(base_dir, "app_icons")
os.makedirs(app_dir, exist_ok=True)
app_img = draw_primary_p_icon(1024)
app_img.save(os.path.join(app_dir, "PureTask_AppIcon_1024_white.png"))
app_img.resize((512,512), Image.LANCZOS).save(os.path.join(app_dir, "PureTask_AppIcon_512_white.png"))
app_img.resize((256,256), Image.LANCZOS).save(os.path.join(app_dir, "PureTask_AppIcon_256_white.png"))
app_img.resize((128,128), Image.LANCZOS).save(os.path.join(app_dir, "PureTask_AppIcon_128_white.png"))

# Include previously generated preview sheets if present
existing_imgs = []
for fname in os.listdir("/mnt/data"):
    if fname.endswith(".png") and ("PureTas" in fname or "logo" in fname or "vector_image_displays_three_variations" in fname):
        existing_imgs.append(os.path.join("/mnt/data", fname))

# Create a simple Brand Guide PDF
pdf_path = os.path.join(base_dir, "PureTask_BrandGuide.pdf")
c = canvas.Canvas(pdf_path, pagesize=LETTER)
w, h = LETTER
c.setTitle("PureTask Brand Guide")
c.setFont("Helvetica-Bold", 20)
c.drawString(1*inch, h-1.2*inch, "PureTask – Brand Guide (v1)")

c.setFont("Helvetica", 12)
c.drawString(1*inch, h-1.6*inch, "Primary Logo: Rounded Minimal 'P' + 'PureTask' wordmark (rounded, mixed case)")
c.drawString(1*inch, h-1.9*inch, "Color Palette:")
c.setFillColorRGB(0/255,92/255,255/255); c.rect(1*inch, h-2.4*inch, 0.7*inch, 0.3*inch, fill=1)
c.setFillColorRGB(47/255,231/255,214/255); c.rect(1.8*inch, h-2.4*inch, 0.7*inch, 0.3*inch, fill=1)
c.setFillColorRGB(249/255,199/255,79/255); c.rect(2.6*inch, h-2.4*inch, 0.7*inch, 0.3*inch, fill=1)
c.setFillColorRGB(1,1,1); c.setStrokeColorRGB(0.2,0.2,0.2); c.rect(3.4*inch, h-2.4*inch, 0.7*inch, 0.3*inch, fill=1, stroke=1)
c.setFillColorRGB(0.04,0.09,0.165); c.rect(4.2*inch, h-2.4*inch, 0.7*inch, 0.3*inch, fill=1)

c.setFillColorRGB(0,0,0)
c.drawString(1*inch, h-2.75*inch, f"Royal Blue {ROYAL_BLUE} • Aqua {AQUA} • Gold {GOLD} • White {WHITE} • Navy {NAVY}")

body = textwrap.fill(
    "Usage: Prefer gradient icon on digital surfaces, flat blue icon for print and small sizes. "
    "Maintain clear space around the logo equal to the height of the 'P' inner counter. "
    "Do not rotate, skew, apply drop shadows, or change colors arbitrarily. "
    "App icon uses white background with the rounded 'P' in Royal Blue.",
    width=90
)
textobj = c.beginText(1*inch, h-3.3*inch)
textobj.setFont("Helvetica", 12)
for line in body.splitlines():
    textobj.textLine(line)
c.drawText(textobj)

c.showPage()
c.save()

# Build ZIP file
zip_path = "/mnt/data/PureTask_LogoPackage.zip"
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
    # add svg assets
    for fname in os.listdir(base_dir):
        fp = os.path.join(base_dir, fname)
        if os.path.isfile(fp) and (fname.endswith(".svg") or fname.endswith(".pdf")):
            z.write(fp, arcname=f"PureTask_LogoAssets/{fname}")
    # add app icons
    for fname in os.listdir(app_dir):
        z.write(os.path.join(app_dir, fname), arcname=f"PureTask_LogoAssets/app_icons/{fname}")
    # add existing preview images
    for fp in existing_imgs:
        z.write(fp, arcname=f"PureTask_LogoAssets/previews/{os.path.basename(fp)}")

zip_path

    return '</svg>'

def gradient_def(id_="grad1", start=ROYAL_BLUE, end=AQUA):
    return f'''
    <defs>
      <linearGradient id="{id_}" x1="0" y1="0" x2="1" y2="1">
        <stop offset="0%" stop-color="{start}"/>
        <stop offset="100%" stop-color="{end}"/>
      </linearGradient>
    </defs>
    '''

    return f'''

      <path d="M128,48 h80 a48,48 0 0 1 0,96 h-80 z" fill="{WHITE}"/>
    </g>
    '''

# Create white background app icon PNG (rounded style primary)
app_dir = os.path.join(base_dir, "app_icons")

def draw_primary_p_icon(img_size=1024):
    img = Image.new("RGBA", (img_size, img_size), (255,255,255,255))
    draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)
    # stem
    stem_x, stem_y, stem_w, stem_h, r = int(img_size*0.35), int(img_size*0.2), int(img_size*0.18), int(img_size*0.6), int(img_size*0.08)
    draw.rounded_rectangle((stem_x, stem_y, stem_x+stem_w, stem_y+stem_h), r, fill=(0,92,255,255))
    # bowl outer
    bowl_x, bowl_y, bowl_w, bowl_h = stem_x+stem_w, stem_y, int(img_size*0.26), int(img_size*0.19)
    draw.rounded_rectangle((bowl_x, bowl_y, bowl_x+bowl_w, bowl_y+bowl_h), int(img_size*0.09), fill=(0,92,255,255))
    # inner knockout
    inner_x, inner_y, inner_w, inner_h = bowl_x+int(img_size*0.04), bowl_y+int(img_size*0.04), int(img_size*0.18), int(img_size*0.11)
    draw.rounded_rectangle((inner_x, inner_y, inner_x+inner_w, inner_y+inner_h), int(img_size*0.06), fill=(255,255,255,255))
    return img

app_img = draw_primary_p_icon(1024)

for fname in os.listdir("/mnt/data"):
    if fname.endswith(".png") and ("PureTas" in fname or "logo" in fname or "vector_image_displays_three_variations" in fname):
        os.link(os.path.join("/mnt/data", fname), os.path.join(previews_dir, fname))

# Zip everything
zip_path = "/mnt/data/PureTask_LogoPackage_v2.zip"
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
    for root, _, files in os.walk(base_dir):
        for f in files:
            full = os.path.join(root, f)
            arc = os.path.relpath(full, start="/mnt/data")
            z.write(full, arcname=arc)

  <defs>
    <linearGradient id="pt-grad" x1="0" y1="0" x2="1" y2="1">
      <stop offset="0%" stop-color="#005CFF"/>
      <stop offset="100%" stop-color="#2FE7D6"/>
    </linearGradient>
  </defs>
  <!-- stem -->
  <rect x="128" y="64" width="96" height="320" rx="48" ry="48" fill="url(#pt-grad)"/>
  <!-- bowl -->
  <path d="M224,64 h128 a96,96 0 0 1 0,192 h-128 z" fill="url(#pt-grad)"/>
  <!-- inner counter -->
  <path d="M256,112 h80 a48,48 0 0 1 0,96 h-80 z" fill="#FFFFFF"/>
</svg>
